# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

Use `sg_list_repos` to discover available repositories before searching.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

## Your Task

Find all C++ source files in envoyproxy/envoy that implement dynamic cluster discovery and health checking: the CDS (Cluster Discovery Service) subscription, the cluster manager update logic, the active health check scheduling, and the outlier detection integration.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:

interconnected subsystems:\\n\\n## Cluster Discovery Service (CDS)\\n\\nThe CDS implementation is centered in `source/common/upstream/` where:\\n- `cds_api_impl.cc/h` implements the core CDS subscription mechanism, extending `Envoy::Config::SubscriptionBase<envoy::config::cluster::v3::Cluster>` and managing cluster discovery requests through gRPC\\n- `cds_api_helper.cc/h` provides a helper class that handles configuration updates from the subscription, processing added and removed clusters\\n- `od_cds_api_impl.cc/h` implements On-Demand CDS (ODCDS) for dynamic cluster discovery on-demand, supporting lazy cluster loading\\n- `cluster_discovery_manager.cc/h` manages the overall cluster discovery workflow\\n\\n## Cluster Manager Integration\\n\\nThe cluster manager coordinates cluster lifecycle and updates:\\n- `cluster_manager_impl.cc/h` is the central cluster management implementation that orchestrates CDS subscriptions, creates and manages cluster instances, handles cluster initialization, and manages thread-local updates\\n- `cluster_factory_impl.cc/h` creates cluster instances with proper health checkers and load balancers configured\\n- `cluster_update_tracker.cc/h` tracks cluster updates via callbacks from the cluster manager\\n\\n## Active Health Checking\\n\\nHealth checking is implemented across multiple layers:\\n\\n**Core Health Checker Framework:**\\n- `health_checker_impl.cc/h` provides the base active health checker implementation, managing health check sessions and scheduling\\n- `health_checker_event_logger.cc/h` logs health checking events for debugging and observability\\n- `health_discovery_service.cc/h` implements the gRPC health discovery service for remote health status reporting\\n\\n**Health Checker Extensions:**\\n- `source/extensions/health_checkers/common/health_checker_base_impl.cc/h` provides the base implementation for all health checker types\\n- `source/extensions/health_checkers/http/health_checker_impl.cc/h` implements HTTP health checking with request/response validation\\n- `source/extensions/health_checkers/tcp/health_checker_impl.cc/h` implements TCP health checking with connection validation\\n- `source/extensions/health_checkers/grpc/health_checker_impl.cc/h` implements gRPC health checking using the standard gRPC health check protocol\\n- `source/extensions/health_checkers/redis/redis.cc/h` implements Redis-specific health checking\\n- `source/extensions/health_checkers/thrift/thrift.cc/h` implements Thrift health checking\\n\\n**Health Checker Integration:**\\n- `upstream_impl.cc/h` contains the `ClusterImplBase::setHealthChecker()` method that integrates health checkers with cluster instances\\n\\n## Outlier Detection Integration\\n\\n- `outlier_detection_impl.cc/h` implements outlier detection that tracks host health and ejects unhealthy hosts based on configured detection algorithms\\n- Outlier detection integrates with the health checking system to mark hosts as ejected when thresholds are exceeded\\n\\n## gRPC/XDS Configuration Subscription\\n\\nCDS is delivered through gRPC subscriptions implemented in `source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/`:\\n\\n**Subscription Management:**\\n- `grpc_subscription_impl.cc/h` provides the gRPC subscription implementation for any resource type\\n- `grpc_subscription_factory.cc/h` creates subscription instances for different resource types\\n\\n**gRPC Mux Implementation (Legacy):**\\n- `grpc_mux_impl.cc/h` implements the original gRPC multiplexer for aggregated discovery service (ADS)\\n- `new_grpc_mux_impl.cc/h` provides an improved implementation with better resource caching and management\\n\\n**XDS Mux (Modern Implementation):**\\n- `xds_mux/grpc_mux_impl.cc/h` implements the XDS protocol mux for handling multiple resource types\\n- `xds_mux/sotw_subscription_state.cc/h` manages State-of-the-World (SotW) subscription state\\n- `xds_mux/delta_subscription_state.cc/h` manages Delta subscription state for incremental updates\\n- `xds_mux/subscription_state.h` defines the subscription state interface\\n\\n**Supporting Infrastructure:**\\n- `grpc_collection_subscription_factory.cc/h` handles aggregated collection subscriptions\\n- `watch_map.cc/h` manages watches for different resource types\\n- `pausable_ack_queue.cc/h` implements acknowledgment queue management with pause/resume capability\\n- `delta_subscription_state.cc/h` and related files handle delta subscription state\\n- `eds_resources_cache_impl.cc/h` caches Endpoint Discovery Service (EDS) resources for efficient memory usage\\n- `grpc_mux_context.h` provides context for gRPC mux implementations\\n- `grpc_stream.h` and `grpc_stream_interface.h` define the streaming protocol\\n- `xds_source_id.cc/h` manages XDS source identifiers\\n- `update_ack.h` defines acknowledgment structures\\n\\n## Load Stats Reporting\\n\\n- `load_stats_reporter.cc/h` implements reporting of load and resource statistics back to the control plane through the Load Reporting Service (LRS)\\n\\nThese files collectively implement Envoy's dynamic cluster discovery through CDS subscriptions, active health checking of cluster endpoints with multiple protocol support (HTTP, gRPC, TCP, Redis, Thrift), outlier detection integration for automatic host ejection, and the complete gRPC/XDS control plane communication infrastructure.\"\n}\n",

interconnected subsystems:\\n\\n## Cluster Discovery Service (CDS)\\n\\nThe CDS implementation is centered in `source/common/upstream/` where:\\n- `cds_api_impl.cc/h` implements the core CDS subscription mechanism, extending `Envoy::Config::SubscriptionBase<envoy::config::cluster::v3::Cluster>` and managing cluster discovery requests through gRPC\\n- `cds_api_helper.cc/h` provides a helper class that handles configuration updates from the subscription, processing added and removed clusters\\n- `od_cds_api_impl.cc/h` implements On-Demand CDS (ODCDS) for dynamic cluster discovery on-demand, supporting lazy cluster loading\\n- `cluster_discovery_manager.cc/h` manages the overall cluster discovery workflow\\n\\n## Cluster Manager Integration\\n\\nThe cluster manager coordinates cluster lifecycle and updates:\\n- `cluster_manager_impl.cc/h` is the central cluster management implementation that orchestrates CDS subscriptions, creates and manages cluster instances, handles cluster initialization, and manages thread-local updates\\n- `cluster_factory_impl.cc/h` creates cluster instances with proper health checkers and load balancers configured\\n- `cluster_update_tracker.cc/h` tracks cluster updates via callbacks from the cluster manager\\n\\n## Active Health Checking\\n\\nHealth checking is implemented across multiple layers:\\n\\n**Core Health Checker Framework:**\\n- `health_checker_impl.cc/h` provides the base active health checker implementation, managing health check sessions and scheduling\\n- `health_checker_event_logger.cc/h` logs health checking events for debugging and observability\\n- `health_discovery_service.cc/h` implements the gRPC health discovery service for remote health status reporting\\n\\n**Health Checker Extensions:**\\n- `source/extensions/health_checkers/common/health_checker_base_impl.cc/h` provides the base implementation for all health checker types\\n- `source/extensions/health_checkers/http/health_checker_impl.cc/h` implements HTTP health checking with request/response validation\\n- `source/extensions/health_checkers/tcp/health_checker_impl.cc/h` implements TCP health checking with connection validation\\n- `source/extensions/health_checkers/grpc/health_checker_impl.cc/h` implements gRPC health checking using the standard gRPC health check protocol\\n- `source/extensions/health_checkers/redis/redis.cc/h` implements Redis-specific health checking\\n- `source/extensions/health_checkers/thrift/thrift.cc/h` implements Thrift health checking\\n\\n**Health Checker Integration:**\\n- `upstream_impl.cc/h` contains the `ClusterImplBase::setHealthChecker()` method that integrates health checkers with cluster instances\\n\\n## Outlier Detection Integration\\n\\n- `outlier_detection_impl.cc/h` implements outlier detection that tracks host health and ejects unhealthy hosts based on configured detection algorithms\\n- Outlier detection integrates with the health checking system to mark hosts as ejected when thresholds are exceeded\\n\\n## gRPC/XDS Configuration Subscription\\n\\nCDS is delivered through gRPC subscriptions implemented in `source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/`:\\n\\n**Subscription Management:**\\n- `grpc_subscription_impl.cc/h` provides the gRPC subscription implementation for any resource type\\n- `grpc_subscription_factory.cc/h` creates subscription instances for different resource types\\n\\n**gRPC Mux Implementation (Legacy):**\\n- `grpc_mux_impl.cc/h` implements the original gRPC multiplexer for aggregated discovery service (ADS)\\n- `new_grpc_mux_impl.cc/h` provides an improved implementation with better resource caching and management\\n\\n**XDS Mux (Modern Implementation):**\\n- `xds_mux/grpc_mux_impl.cc/h` implements the XDS protocol mux for handling multiple resource types\\n- `xds_mux/sotw_subscription_state.cc/h` manages State-of-the-World (SotW) subscription state\\n- `xds_mux/delta_subscription_state.cc/h` manages Delta subscription state for incremental updates\\n- `xds_mux/subscription_state.h` defines the subscription state interface\\n\\n**Supporting Infrastructure:**\\n- `grpc_collection_subscription_factory.cc/h` handles aggregated collection subscriptions\\n- `watch_map.cc/h` manages watches for different resource types\\n- `pausable_ack_queue.cc/h` implements acknowledgment queue management with pause/resume capability\\n- `delta_subscription_state.cc/h` and related files handle delta subscription state\\n- `eds_resources_cache_impl.cc/h` caches Endpoint Discovery Service (EDS) resources for efficient memory usage\\n- `grpc_mux_context.h` provides context for gRPC mux implementations\\n- `grpc_stream.h` and `grpc_stream_interface.h` define the streaming protocol\\n- `xds_source_id.cc/h` manages XDS source identifiers\\n- `update_ack.h` defines acknowledgment structures\\n\\n## Load Stats Reporting\\n\\n- `load_stats_reporter.cc/h` implements reporting of load and resource statistics back to the control plane through the Load Reporting Service (LRS)\\n\\nThese files collectively implement Envoy's dynamic cluster discovery through CDS subscriptions, active health checking of cluster endpoints with multiple protocol support (HTTP, gRPC, TCP, Redis, Thrift), outlier detection integration for automatic host ejection, and the complete gRPC/XDS control plane communication infrastructure.\"\n}\n",
